 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right">Exhibit 99.1 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:13pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">Microsoft Cloud Powers Record Fourth Quarter Results </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>REDMOND, Wash. &#151; July</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;18, 2019 &#151;
</B>Microsoft Corp. today announced the following results for the quarter ended June&nbsp;30, 2019, as compared to the corresponding period of last fiscal year: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Revenue was $33.7&nbsp;billion and increased 12% </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Operating income was $12.4&nbsp;billion and increased 20% </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>

innovating with them, creating new businesses with them, and earning their trust. This commitment to our customers&#146; success is resulting in larger, multi-year commercial cloud agreements and growing momentum across every layer of our technology

<TD VALIGN="bottom" STYLE="BORDER-BOTTOM:1px solid #000000"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&nbsp;</FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" STYLE="BORDER-BOTTOM:1px solid #000000"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#666666">22%</FONT></P></TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom" STYLE="BORDER-BOTTOM:1px solid #000000"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&nbsp;</FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" STYLE=" BORDER-BOTTOM:1px solid #000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" STYLE="BORDER-BOTTOM:1px solid #000000"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&nbsp;</FONT></P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" STYLE="BORDER-BOTTOM:1px solid #000000"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#666666">23%</FONT></P></TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom" STYLE="BORDER-BOTTOM:1px solid #000000"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; line-height:14pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&nbsp;</FONT></P></TD></TR>
</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">The current year effective tax rate was 10% and 16% on a GAAP and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT>
basis, respectively. GAAP results include a net income tax benefit of $2.6&nbsp;billion and a net income tax charge of $157&nbsp;million for the twelve months ended June&nbsp;30, 2019. GAAP results include a net income tax charge of
$13.7&nbsp;billion for the twelve months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018. These net tax impacts are excluded from our <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> results and explained in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Definition
section below<B>.</B> </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Business Outlook </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft will provide forward-looking guidance in connection with this quarterly earnings announcement on its earnings conference call and
webcast. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Quarterly Highlights, Product Releases, and Enhancements</B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Every quarter Microsoft delivers hundreds of products, either as new releases, services, or enhancements to current products and services. These
releases are a result of significant research and development investments, made over multiple years, designed to help customers be more productive and secure and to deliver differentiated value across the cloud and the edge. </FONT></P>
</DIV></Center>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Here are the <U>major product releases and other highlights</U> for the quarter, organized by
product categories, to help illustrate how we are accelerating innovation across our businesses while expanding our market opportunities. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666"><B>Webcast Details </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Satya Nadella, chief executive officer, Amy Hood, executive vice president and chief financial
officer, Frank Brod, chief accounting officer, Keith Dolliver, deputy general counsel, and Michael Spencer, general manager of investor relations, will host a conference call and webcast at 2:30 p.m. Pacific time (5:30 p.m. Eastern time) today to
discuss details of the company&#146;s performance for the quarter and certain forward-looking information. The session may be accessed at <U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">http://www.microsoft.com/en-us/investor</FONT></U>. The webcast will be
available for replay through the close of business on July&nbsp;18, 2020. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT>
Definition </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><I>Transfer of Intangible Properties</I>. In the fourth quarter of fiscal year 2019, in response to the TCJA and
recently issued regulations, we transferred certain intangible properties held by our foreign subsidiaries to the United States and Ireland. The transfers of intangible properties resulted in a net $2.6&nbsp;billion tax benefit recorded in the
fourth quarter of fiscal year 2019, as the value of future tax deductions exceeded the current tax liability from foreign jurisdictions and United States Global Intangible <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Low-Taxed</FONT> Income (GILTI) tax.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><I>The TCJA Impact</I>. We recorded a net charge of $157&nbsp;million during the twelve months ended June&nbsp;30, 2019 related to the
TCJA. We recorded a net benefit of $104&nbsp;million during the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018 and a net charge of $13.7&nbsp;billion during the twelve months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018 related to the TCJA. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">We have provided <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures related to the transfer of intangible properties and the TCJA
to aid investors in better understanding our performance. We believe these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures assist investors by providing additional insight into our operational performance and help clarify trends affecting
our business. For comparability of reporting, management considers <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures in conjunction with GAAP financial results in evaluating business performance. The
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented in this release should not be considered as a substitute for, or superior to, the measures of financial performance prepared in accordance with GAAP. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Constant Currency </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft presents constant currency information to provide a framework for assessing how our underlying businesses performed excluding the effect
of foreign currency rate fluctuations. To present this information, current and comparative prior period results for entities reporting in currencies other than United States dollars are converted into United States dollars using the average
exchange rates from the comparative period rather than the actual exchange rates in effect during the respective periods. All growth comparisons relate to the corresponding period in the last fiscal year. Microsoft has provided this <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial information to aid investors in better understanding our performance. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented in this release should not be considered as
a substitute for, or superior to, the measures of financial performance prepared in accordance with GAAP. </FONT></P>
</DIV></Center>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>MICROSOFT CORPORATION </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>FOURTH QUARTER FINANCIAL HIGHLIGHTS </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">All growth comparisons relate to the corresponding period in the last fiscal year. Please refer to the reconciliation of our GAAP and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial results in the table provided above for
additional information. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>SUMMARY </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">Revenue was $33.7&nbsp;billion and increased 12%, driven by growth across each of our segments. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Gross margin was
$23.3&nbsp;billion and increased 15%, driven by growth across each of our segments. Gross margin percentage increased, driven by gross margin percentage improvement in More Personal Computing and Productivity and Business Processes, and favorable
segment sales mix. Gross margin included a 6 percentage point improvement in commercial cloud, primarily from Azure. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Operating income
was $12.4&nbsp;billion and increased 20%, driven by growth across each of our segments. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Net income was $13.2&nbsp;billion and
increased 49%. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> net income was $10.6&nbsp;billion and increased 21%, excluding the net $2.6&nbsp;billion income tax benefit in the current year and the net $104&nbsp;million income tax benefit in the
prior year. These net tax benefits are explained in the Income Taxes section below. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Diluted earnings per share was $1.71 and increased
50%. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> diluted earnings per share was $1.37 and increased 21%, excluding $0.34 related to the net tax benefit in the current year and $0.01 related to the net tax benefit in the prior year. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Revenue, gross margin, and operating income included an unfavorable foreign currency impact of 2%, 2%, and 4%, respectively. </FONT></P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>INCOME TAXES </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">The current quarter effective tax rate was (5)% and 16% on a GAAP and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> basis, respectively,
compared to 17% and 18% in the prior year. GAAP results include a net income tax benefit of $2.6&nbsp;billion related to intangible property transfers for the fourth quarter of fiscal year 2019 and a net income tax benefit of $104&nbsp;million
related to the TCJA for the fourth quarter of fiscal year 2018. These net tax benefits are excluded from our <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> results. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">In the fourth quarter of fiscal year 2019, in response to the TCJA and recently issued regulations, we transferred certain intangible properties
held by our foreign subsidiaries to the United States and Ireland. The transfers of intangible properties resulted in a net $2.6&nbsp;billion tax benefit recorded in the fourth quarter of fiscal year 2019, as the value of future tax deductions
exceeded the current tax liability from foreign jurisdictions and United States GILTI tax. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>CONTRACTED NOT RECOGNIZED REVENUE
</B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Contracted not recognized revenue, which includes unearned revenue and amounts that will be invoiced and recognized as revenue in
future periods, was $91&nbsp;billion as of June&nbsp;30, 2019, an increase of 25% over the prior year. We expect to recognize approximately 50% of this revenue over the next 12 months and the remainder thereafter. Many customers are committing to
our products and services for longer contract terms, which is increasing the percentage of contracted revenue that will be recognized beyond the next 12 months. </FONT></P>
</DIV></Center>
